# Research Log

Daily pre-market research entries are appended below by the `pre-market` routine.

## Entry Schema

```
## YYYY-MM-DD — Pre-market Research

### Account
- Equity: $X
- Cash: $X
- Buying power: $X
- Daytrade count: N

### Market Context
- WTI / Brent oil:
- S&P 500 futures:
- VIX:
- Today's catalysts:
- Earnings before open:
- Economic calendar:
- Sector momentum:

### Trade Ideas
Listed in R:R-descending order (tie-break: ticker ascending). One numbered line per idea, format:
1. **ID:** `pm-YYYY-MM-DD-TICKER` — TICKER, catalyst, entry $X, stop $X, target $X, R:R X:1, planned trail percent: 10
2. ...

### Risk Factors
- ...

### Decision
TRADE or HOLD (default HOLD if no edge)

### Sources
- Perplexity citations: <list>
- WebSearch fallback used: yes/no (which queries)
```

---

## 2026-04-27 — Pre-market Research (refreshed)

*Prior 2026-04-27 entry refreshed: corrected SPX futures level, added FOMC Wed Apr 29 + Big Tech earnings (MSFT/GOOG) Wed which were missing from prior version. Original preserved in git history (commit abf37e7).*

### Account
- Equity: $10,000.00
- Cash: $10,000.00
- Buying power: $20,000.00
- Daytrade count: 0
- Positions: none | Open orders: none
- Note: Alpaca account shows `options_trading_level: 3` — irrelevant per hard rule "NO OPTIONS, ever"; wrapper kill-switch + buy-side gate (stocks only) prevent any options path.

### Market Context
- WTI: ~$92–94/bbl (Apr 23 close ~$92.92; prediction markets imply ~$94 today). Brent: not directly quoted today; recent ~$105 area, softer on supply talk.
- S&P 500 futures: E-mini ~6,865 area in premarket (+2 pts); SPX cash 6,824.66 last close after 7-day up streak. Premarket flat-to-slightly-up. NDX futures +48, Dow futures -2.
- VIX: 19.31 (Apr 23 close), range 18.87–19.50 — calm regime.
- Today's catalysts: Dallas Fed Manufacturing Survey 10:30 AM ET. VZ earnings BMO. Otherwise light.
- Earnings before open: VZ (Verizon) is the marquee BMO name; smaller: SSYS (Stratasys), BH (Biglari), GWRS, UFI, EARN. After close: minor.
- This-week event risk (high): **FOMC statement + Powell presser Wed Apr 29 (2:00 / 2:30 PM ET)**; **MSFT + GOOG earnings Wed Apr 29 (most likely AMC)**; META/AMZN/AAPL likely later in week; ECI Q1 Thu Apr 30.
- 10Y yield: 4.289% (~unch). Crude/Brent/natgas softer overnight.
- Sector momentum YTD (recent reads): Energy leading (~+26% YTD, oil-firm + AI-power demand); Industrials #2 (~+9–16%, defense/AI infra); Consumer Staples #3 (~+10%); Tech/Semis still strong with IT +45% forward EPS revisions.

### Trade Ideas
*(v1 paper — kill-switch active, documentation only; verify live prices at v2 market-open before any entry. With FOMC + Big Tech earnings Wed, prudent stance is to defer fresh entries until post-event.)*

1. **XLE** — Energy sector remains YTD leader; oil firm in low-$90s; non-binary, sector-ETF avoids single-name event risk. Indicative entry ~$95, stop ~$85.50 (-10%), target ~$114 (+20%), R:R ~2:1.
2. **XLI** — Industrials #2 YTD; defense + AI-infrastructure tailwind, not directly exposed to MSFT/GOOG print. Indicative entry ~$160, stop ~$144 (-10%), target ~$192 (+20%), R:R ~2:1.
3. **SMH** — Semis broad ETF; AI capex thesis intact, but **carries indirect Big-Tech-earnings spillover Wed**. Indicative entry ~$295, stop ~$265.50 (-10%), target ~$354 (+20%), R:R ~2:1. Prefer waiting until after MSFT/GOOG print.

Buy-side gate (forward check): all three pass position count (0/6), trades-this-week (0/3), 20%-cap, sector-momentum, stock-only. Final cash / PDT check belongs at execution.

### Risk Factors
- **Macro / event:** FOMC Wed is the dominant risk; any hawkish surprise hits multiples broadly. Powell tone matters more than statement.
- **Earnings concentration:** ~40% of S&P 500 market cap reports this week; MSFT/GOOG Wed dictate sentiment for tech and semis.
- **Sector:** Energy headline risk if US–Iran/OPEC+ talk deflates oil; semis stretched after multi-quarter run.
- **Idiosyncratic:** Single-name high-priced AI plays (AVGO, etc.) breach 20% cap on $10K account; favor sector ETFs.
- **Liquidity:** Pre-FOMC, Mon–Tue chop is common; thin conviction trades tend to underperform.

### Decision
**HOLD** — Day 1, v1 paper-only, kill-switch active. Even ignoring the kill-switch, the rational stance is to wait through FOMC (Wed) and Big Tech prints before deploying capital. Patience > activity.

### Decision
**TRADE** — 1 satellite idea (GE) confirmed; XLK deferred.

Rationale: (1) **GE 50s-RS matured** — Tue's razor-thin +0.60pp expanded to +3.82pp Fri PM through hot-CPI Wed + friendly-PPI Thu binary cycle = durable regime confirmation (the v3 deferral path validated yesterday's HOLD and today's TRADE); (2) **GE held through binaries while NVDA/AVGO worsened** — clear relative-strength demonstration on the same window (GE 10s +3.72% vs NVDA −4.27% vs AVGO −9.61%); (3) **Industrials sector leading-quadrant unchanged** — XLI +3.46% Thu, sector rotation intact; (4) **All buy-side gates pass with margin** — position $1,331 = 13.30% equity, core floor 65.34% post-fill, Industrials 2/2 satellites at cap, 0/5 weekly trades remaining; (5) **VIX compressed to 19.44** from 22.22 CPI-peak — vol regime stepping back down, spreads/whip risk normalizing; (6) **Patience > activity tradeoff:** v3 was designed to capture exactly this single-stock setup — confirmed RS through binary cycle is the high-conviction signal we deferred Wed pre-print to await; deferring further into FOMC adds binary-stacking without further information gain on GE-specific thesis.

Counter-rationale (acknowledged risks): (a) Industrials concentration 56% of deployed post-fill is material — Rule 10 sector-kill on Industrials would trigger a 3-position liquidation; (b) FOMC Jun 17 binary 3 sessions out — Mon/Tue tape + binary day before lockout; (c) Friday/weekend gap risk; (d) XLE cushion 2.20% on independent oil-tape risk. Satellite slots **2/2 at cap** (CAT + GE — no re-add available). A Rule 10 sector-kill on Industrials would close 3 positions simultaneously. Mitigation: today's Empire State manufacturing print could surprise positive (TradingEconomics already shows 19.60 actual vs 12 consensus = **+58% surprise** if confirmed — directly bullish for Industrials/CAT/GE/XLI).
- **Capital deployment 87.55% — above 75–85% target band:** Post-Fri GE entry overshoot carries into Mon. Adding BTSG ($1,328) would push deployment to **$10,193 / $10,126 = 100.66%** (would breach buying-power-as-100% threshold — must reject the buy on cash check; cash $1,261 < $1,328 needed). **Sizing math fails the cash gate.** Recompute below in Decision rationale.
- **BTSG ADV thin at $197M:** Smallest in screen — adequate for $1.3k satellite slice but limits scale-out responsiveness if Rule 8 ladder triggers; also reduces stale-quote tolerance at open. Mitigation: 15% stop width is wider than CAT (10%) and matches GE (15%) — reflects small-cap vol regime + thin-liquidity allowance.
- **Macro/oil-tape risk independent of XLE-held position:** Even if XLE trails out today, oil shock can ripple Materials (XLB Industrials-input demand) and broad cyclicals (Industrials — GE/CAT/XLI). Defensive bid plausible. Mitigation: ETF core + risk-parity sized satellites bound max loss per position to ~2% equity.
- **Empire State Manufacturing time / actual ambiguity:** Multiple sources contradict on release time AND whether actual already-printed at 19.60. If pre-released and already digested in S&P futures +1.21%, then "no surprise" intraday; if delayed to 12:30 ET / 1:15 PM, the print is still pending. Recommend treating Empire State as pending-binary until first market data confirms.
- **VIX expected-move for Jun 17 expiry ±1.77 (9.26%):** market is pricing FOMC-binary vol expansion. Realized vol post-FOMC could see VIX print 20–22 (similar to CPI Wed Jun 10). Held-book stops at 10–7% trail are well wider than this implied move.
- **Held book idiosyncratic:** CAT cushion 8.98% / GE 12.03% / XLB 7.64% / XLE **1.19% — book's tightest, in active gap-down zone** / XLI 10.65%. XLB cushion is below 10% by Rule 8 design (locked 7% trail at Fri's +4.26% ladder fire). All clear of Rule 6 trigger except XLE which is acute.

### Decision
**HOLD** — defer BTSG to post-FOMC Thursday re-screen.

Rationale: (1) **Cash gate fails on BTSG sizing math** — cash $1,261.00 < required cost $1,327.83 (post-Fri GE entry left only $1,261 cash; cannot buy 21 sh of BTSG at limit-with-slippage cost). Even at 20 sh = $1,264.60 limit would marginally fail $1,261 cash unless slippage favorable; the gate (d) "position cost ≤ available cash" rejects the order in market-open. Documented here so v2 market-open routine doesn't attempt and exit-4 on cash check. (2) **Pre-FOMC binary 2 sessions out + new Fed Chair Warsh first presser** — binary-stacking risk material; deferring BTSG 3 sessions (Mon → Thu) costs 0.5pp of expected 10s-RS but removes binary tail-risk. (3) **XLE 1.19% cushion in active oil-shock gap** — book may auto-exit Energy today; cleaner to assess post-stop-fire (or post-recovery) before adding a new satellite to a potentially shrinking deployed base. (4) **Industrials 54.7% concentration with 2/2 satellite cap** — no GE/CAT re-add available; **BTSG would be sector-diversifying** (Healthcare = 0 current exposure) IF gates passed, which they don't. (5) **Capital deployment 87.55% — already above 75–85% band**; adding BTSG would push to ~100% breaching cash-gate hard. (6) **Patience > activity (Rule 12)** — Week 7 closed 1/5 trades with +1.234% week-P&L; v3 weekly-cap raised to 5 doesn't mandate filling it; carryforwards are how v3 captures setups that mature.

Counter-rationale (acknowledged tradeoffs): (a) BTSG 10s-RS +4.46pp matured this week, defer cost = unknown but BTSG has been running 60% YTD so further upside is statistically the more probable path; (b) XLE auto-exit would free ~$1,910 cash and improve BTSG cash-gate position from Tuesday onward — but Tuesday is FOMC eve, even worse for binary timing; (c) Empire State manufacturing if confirmed 19.60 actual is a Industrials-bullish print → could re-screen CAT/GE/XLI for any ladder-tighten triggers at midday. Net: cash gate fails, FOMC binary 2 sessions out, XLE acute risk. HOLD.

Carry-forward to Tue Jun 16 pre-market re-screen:
- `pm-2026-06-15-BTSG` — **PRIMARY** carryforward (satellite, Healthcare) — 1st-fail = cash gate (recheck if XLE auto-exits or cash budget shifts) + FOMC binary timing (post-FOMC Thursday is the cleaner window).
- `pm-2026-06-15-XLK` — defer further (core, Tech ETF) — 10s-RS reverted to −1.31pp, sector-rotation flagged lagging. Re-arm contingent on +1pp 10s-RS turn AND leading-quadrant flip.
- `pm-2026-06-15-NVDA` — defer (satellite, Tech) — 10s-RS −0.76pp (improved) + 50-DMA breach widened. Both legs needed.
- `pm-2026-06-15-DELL` — **NEW** defer (satellite, Tech AI-infra) — 50s +134% parabolic but 10s-RS −4.07pp on 2-week cool-down. Re-screen post-FOMC for 10s-RS turn.

Market-open: no orders to place (HOLD). Midday: evaluate Rule 7 hard-close threshold across book (XLE the primary watch — but XLE already below entry, trail-stop is the active risk-control; if XLE trails out at $55.53 that's not a Rule 7 close, it's a Rule 6 stop-exit handled by Alpaca). ### Risk Factors
- **$30B pension rebalance sell Mon/Tue (Jun 29-30) = known near-term headwind** per Goldman's Flood Jun 26 commentary — last 2 trading days of Q2 + H1 carry mechanical equity-sell flow as pensions rebalance away from outperforming stocks back to fixed income. **Pre-open ES +0.67% suggests flow already partially absorbed**, but mid-day weakness Mon-Tue likely; could compress DK entry below $47.82 limit. Flood frames this as **"buying opportunity"** — supports today's TRADE plan if entry executes near limit not gap-up. Mitigant: market-open's limit-with-slippage entry will catch pullback below ask.
- **Thu Jul 2 jobs print = week's primary binary (8:30 ET)** — consensus +100K vs May +172K beat; risk asymmetry skewed toward downside surprise per Hiringlab (long-term unemployment 27.5%, financial-activities -22K MoM) but May's blowout sets up "buy-the-cooling" narrative if 50-150K range. **Adding DK Mon means position rides Tue-Wed pre-jobs into the binary** — but DK's beta is moderate and Energy sector is **least correlated to jobs binary** (oil/refining margins drive DK, not employment data). Stop placed Mon at close = Tue forward-armed.
- **Fri Jun 26 Tech-rout (SPY -0.72% / XLK -3.39% / MCHP -7.05% / HPE -7.04%)** = **sector-rotation signal** away from Tech post-PCE-hot digestion; semis got hit harder than software (MU -3.5%, MCHP -7%, HPE -7%). **Idiosyncratic KLIC bucking trend** (+12.18% 10s) but sector overhang on entire Tech cluster heading into pension rebalance + jobs binary = adds stacking risk. **Avoiding Tech today via DK pick** is intentional risk-mitigation (Energy/refining lowest-correlated sector to Tech rout + jobs binary).
- **XLB stop cushion 4.00%** (book's tightest, 100bps above Rule 9 3% floor) — locked at $49.5783 since Jun 17; XLB sits at $51.64 vs hwm $53.31 (Jun 11). **Materials is Tier-1 YTD leader (+15-17%) but PCE-rate-sensitivity persists** — a -3% XLB day fires the stop. Pension rebalance flow Mon-Tue could pressure broad cyclicals; XLB carries the highest cluster risk in held book.

BTSG (4.83% cushion), GE (5.06%), XLI (4.79%) all within typical 4-7% trail compression — multi-position-stop-fire would unwind ~$300-400 unrealized gains; mitigant: Rule 9 floor + stops as designed.

Catalyst is **moderate, not urgent** — could choose to defer entry by 1 week and re-screen. ### Risk Factors
- **$30B pension rebalance day 2 (Tue) = back-half flow** per Goldman Flood Jun 26 — Mon Jun 29 absorbed cleanly with SPY +1.66% pop (Flood "buying opportunity" thesis confirmed); Tue continuation in pre-open ES +0.07-0.72%. **Risk: mid-day weakness Tue as final flow completes; KLIC entry could compress below $129.06 limit** — market-open limit-with-slippage entry will catch any pullback below ask. **By Wed AM full Q2/H1 close institutional re-positioning complete.**
- **Thu Jul 2 jobs print = week's primary binary (8:30 ET)** — consensus +100K vs May +172K beat; Hiringlab risk asymmetry skewed downside (long-term unemployment 27.5%, financial-activities -22K MoM May) but May's blowout sets up "buy-the-cooling" narrative if 50-150K range. **Adding KLIC Tue means position rides Wed-Thu through ADP/ISM/JOLTS Wed + jobs Thu binary**; KLIC has elevated beta (20 5%+ fluctuations in 12mo per Yahoo) → could move ±5-7% on jobs-cluster surprise. **Tech-sector lopsided sensitivity to jobs binary** — Goldman/Forbes consensus IT sector cooling underperformance has 10s-RS still negative; XLK 10s-RS failing 21st session straight. **Mitigant: stop placed Tue at close = Wed forward-armed before Thu binary.**
- **Iran tensions ESCALATING then DE-ESCALATING (Mon → Tue)** — Carnegie commentary frames as "rising geopolitical tensions" Mon-Jun 30, but Benzinga PreMarket Playbook Jun 30 cites "US-Iran 'Stand Down' Lifting Futures" Tue pre-open. **Direct DK impact (rallied +7.86% Mon, could give back Tue) — but we're NOT in DK so no direct held-book exposure to oil-tape mean-reversion**. Indirect: held XLI (Aerospace & Defense 24-27% of XLI) could see modest pull-back on defense-stock de-escalation read; held GE (Aerospace) ditto. **Mitigant: GE 5.76% stop cushion sufficient buffer for typical defense-name single-day move ±2-3%**.
- **Industrials concentration 44.50% of deployed** — still single largest book risk; ~5.50pp under v3.1 50% sector cap; 1/2 sat slots in sector (GE). **Compounds Aerospace-tail risk** if Iran de-escalation Tue. **Mitigant: KLIC fill diversifies into Tech sector (0/2 sats → 1/2)** — first non-Industrials/Materials/Healthcare sat in book history; sector concentration broadens from 3 sectors (Industrials/Materials/Healthcare) to 4 sectors (+Tech).

BTSG (3.08% cushion — book's tightest, 8bps above Rule 9 3% floor), XLB (2.06% cushion — BELOW Rule 9 3% min for new placements but Rule 9 gates new stops not maintenance, no action) are most vulnerable; multi-position-stop-fire would unwind ~$60-90 unrealized gains. **Mitigant: Rule 9 floor logic + stops as designed; Rule 13 forward-arming gives KLIC stop placement at Tue close**.

### Decision
**TRADE — 1 satellite idea armed (KLIC Tech), 1 deferred-by-chase-flag (DK Energy), 1 carryforward-deferred (XLK Tech-core).**

Rationale: (1) **1 satellite slot OPEN** (2/3 used: GE, BTSG); (2) **KLIC passes ALL v3 satellite gates with strongest stack in screen** (10s-RS +14.12pp ✓ / 50s-RS +56.42pp ✓ / 50-DMA ✓ / 200-DMA ✓); (3) **catalyst stacked**: Q2 EPS beat +17.9% + revenue +49.8% YoY + Q3 guidance $310M ±$20M (+~109% YoY) + B.Riley PT raise + BofA AI semis-equipment FY27-28 outlook raise + Goldman Flood semis-equipment "where everyone is and continues to want to be"; (4) **Tech-sector NEW (0/2 → 1/2 sat slots)** = diversifies book from 3 sectors to 4 sectors (Industrials/Materials/Healthcare → +Tech); (5) **deployment 59.66% → 79.49% post-fill** restores Rule 5 target band (cleanly inside 75-85%); (6) **sector cap, position cap, weekly cap, position-count cap all PASS** by wide margin (sector cap 24.93% < 50%; position 19.82% < 20%; weekly 1/5 < 5; positions 5/6 < 6); (7) **patience-tested across 5-of-6 prior pre-market routines** (Jun 22-26 all HOLD or DK-chase-skip on screen-fail; today first session with sat-slot open AND KLIC catalyst stack confirmed); (8) **Tech-sector relatively cheap post-re-rating** per LinkedIn YTD sector commentary — idiosyncratic strength bucks sector-cool environment; (9) **KLIC no near-term earnings risk** (Q3 ~early Aug); (10) **DK deferred as CHASE** (Mon +7.86% gap + thesis inversion oil-up vs oil-down + Iran-ceasefire reversal Tue risk).

KLIC entry rationale on extended price: **$129.06 is 1-day +3.07% above Fri $125.22, not extended at 1-week or 1-month scale** — Mon's +3% is within normal volatility band, not a "chase" move (KLIC has 20 5%+ moves in 12mo); the chase-flag specifically applies to DK's +7.86% 1-day gap-up (much more extreme).

XLK ETF-core gate-watch (CARRYFORWARD, 21st consecutive session): re-arms if (a) sustained 2-session 10s-RS >+1pp confirmation post-Thu jobs print, OR (b) Tech sector rebid breaks XLK above $190 → 10s-RS expands. **Re-test earliest plausible: Mon Jul 6 pre-market** (post-jobs-binary digestion).

### Decision
**HOLD** — no executable idea today. **XLU** is the standing top-R:R core name but a full clip breaches the 85% deployment ceiling (→88.1%), so market-open skips it and it stays watchlisted (re-arms on the next XLI/BTSG scale-out, stop-out, or equity growth freeing ≥~$323 headroom). **No satellite** — macro-window NOT CLEAR (CPI T+0 today, PPI at T+1) and momentum leaders are semi/tech/biotech sector-cautions. Independently, sitting risk flat through today's CPI (T+0) and tomorrow's PPI (T+1) is the prudent posture. Held book (BTSG/XLB/XLI/XLRE) all above stops, ETF-core 86.2% of deployed, sectors ≤50% — no defensive action needed.
